    <li> Stiff - but do loosen up if bent and rolled a little in the fingers. Well worth the money since overall it saves me so much on lashes - most other lashes cost well over the price I paid for these but since I get (20) pairs for this price I&#x27;d be crazy to pass up this deal. For first timers using fake eyelashes it may be a little nerve racking but here is how I apply..&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;First I hold a fake eyelash up to my eye and try and size it. I cut off the extra amount if they are larger than my eyes (which they are). Then I roll them in my fingers a bit to loosen the lashes up so they aren&#x27;t so stiff feeling / looking. Once I feel like they are flexible enough I apply eyelash glue to them (do not use real glue, and also the eyelash glue does not come in the set - so that will need to be purchased separate). I let the glue sit on the lash for about a minute before trying to apply them to my lashes..this gives the glue time to set. (use tweezers to apply if fingers seem to get in your way). Curling these with a lash curler and applying mascara makes them look more realistic. Good luck!</li>
